Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Description: Ukrainians, the warehouse periode, I was worried about the firing, is irresistible, fuel on їkhn ... war with Ukraine 2022, war with Ukraine Latest news today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, war, when, war With Ukraine in 2022 it will be or not, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['psuh-dopomoga.jpg']

Tags: ['МОЗ']

Category: News

Illustrative photo

Ukrainians are now experiencing a very difficult period, and this is certainly affected by the eager mental health.

Aware of the impact and consequences of the war for the mental health of Ukrainians, the Ministry of Health of the National Health Service of Ukraine introduced a new package "Supporting adults and children with mental disorders on primary levels of help" within the framework of the Medical Guarantee Program.

About it reportsMinistry of Health of Ukraine.

Within the package with the consent of the patient, the doctor will conduct a clinical assessment of the physical standing and mental status. According to the results of screening, the family doctor can be proposed:

  • referral to laboratory and instrumental studies to diagnose or exclude PNRs related to physical health; * Driving a patient to a psychiatrist for diagnosis, diagnosing and providing treatment recommendations(with the consent of the patient); * first psychological help(Moreover, not only the patient, but also the members of his family who care for him/her); * Psychosocial, as well as pharmacological and behavioral interventions, and in the absence of positive dynamics, then referral to a specialist.

If you need psychological assistance, you can also consult your family doctor. He will provide services within his competence and refer to other specialists in razine.

Currently, 252 medical institutions have fulfilled the appropriate conditions and have a contractual provision of medical services.

Finding a medical facility that provides a medical care under the NSAU with a NSSA and can be enrolled in consultation in one way:

  • Call the NSAU Contact Center at 16-77, * Use Dashboard on the NSAU-Choose a package "Supporting and Treatment of Adults and Children with Mental Disorders at the Primary Level of Medical Assistance" in the group of services.

In the coming years, Russia will not be able to produce as much gas as before the war - an expert

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-01T-134:42:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T16:42:00+03:00

Description: In the next few years, Russia will not be able to return to the volume of gas production that have been in a full -scale invasion of Ukraine. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16829..."]

Tags: ['Газ', 'росія']

Type: Article

In the next few years, Russia will not be able to return to the volumes of production, which were to a full -scale invasion of Ukraine.

Olena Pavlenko, President of the Dixigrour Analytical Center, informed in a comment to Ukrinform.

“Reduction of Russian gas exports is a consequence of Russia's behavior that has maintained a response in the European Union. This process has begun, as a simple refusal to buy Russian gas, but will end with the fact that RFF will not be able to return to those volumes for the next few years(extraction - ed.)which she extracted before the war, ”Pavlenko said.

According to her, in 2021, Russia was blackmailing Europe with its gas, and the beginning of a full -scale invasion of the European Union voluntarily to abandon their gas. And this reduction in exports automatically reflected in the domestic production.

Read also: Russian gas Pavlenko called the reasons that influenced the reduction of production. The first is the market because the Chinese market cannot replace the European that does not buy Russian gas. The second - large companies that provided basic investments and technologies were started from gas production.

“That is, they do not have the money to do further with the exploration and drill a new release. And if it is, it is not as scale as it was before, ”the expert emphasized.

In addition, in her opinion, theoretically exports of Russian gas can fall even more than twice, since the European Commission has ambitions at all.

Read also: “Now the Russians are trying to find around. For example, they want to create a so -called "gas hub" with the Turks, where they will be able to sell their gas. And Turkey will already put its box and sell gas further. Thus, Russia will be able to regain part of the market again. The geopolitical conjuncture is not in favor of Gazprom, ”Pavlenko survived.

Ukraine wants to join the Transstikoochean Partnership Agreement

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-01T-136:42:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T16:42:00+03:00

Description: President Volodymyr Zelensky has approved the composition of the delegation to participate in the negotiations on Ukraine's accession to a comprehensive and progressive transitochean partnership agreement. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16829..."]

Tags: ['Транстихоокеанське партнерство', 'Україна', 'Зеленський']

Type: Article

President Volodymyr Zelensky has approved the composition of the delegation for the participation of Ukraine on the accession of Ukraine to the comprehensive and progressive agreement of the Processhoooche Partnership.

The appropriate order is published on , reports Ukrinform.

"To form a delegation of Ukraine to participate in the negotiations on the accession of Ukraine of the Ssesovna and Progressive Agreement on the Transstricocean Partnership," the document states.

The head of the delegation was appointed the first Viceremier-Minister-Minister of Economy Sviridenko. The delegation also included six officials -representatives of the Ministry of Economy, Ministry of Justice, Ministry of Agrarian Policy, State Customs Service of the Presidential Office.

The Head of State also approved the delegation directives, but they have a stamp for service use.

Read also: The Ministry of Economy of Ukraine expects an entry into the Agreement of the Proterantyhooochean Partnership in early 2024, reported in .

«Разом з тим, є перспектива приєднатися до Угоди вже цього року. Це дастьУкраїні можливість лібералізації нетарифних обмежень у торгівлі товарами іпослугам з країнами цього регіону, а також відкриє доступ на нові ринки збуту.Крім того, це надасть нам змогу розширити доступ до прямих іноземнихінвестицій», - зазначила віцепрем’єр-міністр – міністр економіки України ЮліяСвириденко.

Свириденко нагадала, що всеосяжна та прогресивна угода про Транстихоокеанськепартнерство (CPTPP) . As of 2022, it was ratified by eight countries: Australia, Canada, Japan, Mexico, Peru, New Zealand, Singapore and Vietnam. The countries of the Transfoluoe Partnership are mainly exported by electronics, cars, cars and mineral fuels.

February 1 2021 She officially informed 11 CPTPP member states about her intention to join the trading unit.

The French city erected a monument to Anna Yaroslavna

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-01T-16:41:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T23:41:00+03:00

Description: In the city of Le-Blan-Menil, near Paris, a sculpture of young Anna Yaroslavna, Queen of France, was installed. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16829..."]

Tags: ['Анна Ярославна', 'Франція', 'Історія', "Пам'ятник"]

Type: Article

In the city of the Blan-Menil, near Paris, they installed a sculpture of young Annijaroslavna, Queen of France.

The Embassy of Ukraine in France reports this in , reports Ukrinform.

“In Anna's Municipal Park of Kyiv City Le-Blan-Menil(Department of Saint-San)The sculpture of young Anna Kyiv - the daughter of Prince of Kyiv Rus Yaroslav the Wise and Queen of France was established. The city of Le-Blan-Menil became the second French city after the Toulouse, which participates in the international project-"The Way of the Queen", which began in ancient Kiev, when the young daughter of the Great Kievan Rus-Ukraine Yaroslav the Wise Anna went to France and Henry and Henry. ”, - the message says.

The embassy noted that the participants of the project, initiated by author and the founder of the International Festival of Arts Anne de Kyiv Festfedor Balandin with the support of the KSCA, except France, have already become Poland, Czech Republic, Austria, Germany, Belgium and Luxembourg.

The Ukrainian diplomatic mission also noted that the "Way of the Queen" in the city of Le-Blan-Menil was supported by the fact that in 1060, Anna Kyiv royalmus was transferred to the abbot of Sanlis Le-Blan-Menil. The decree, which is first mentioned by Le-Blan-Menil, is the founding act that contributes to the establishment of identity of the city.

Read also: The opening of the sculpture was attended by the adviser to the Embassy of Ukraine in France Victoria Gulenko. She noted that it is currently important to honor the part of the other , especially in these difficult times, when the enemy tries to destroy our historical ties, our memories, noise, rewrite history and get rid of our existence. She also dressed the senator, the mayor of the city and all involved in the support of the Ukrainian Narode and for the worthy place they gave our common history.

It was reported that in June in Paris plan to open the Kiev square.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Tags: ['Канада', 'Операція', 'Польща', 'Україна', 'Травма']

Type: Article

Leading plastic surgeons will operate in a hospital in southern Poland wounded by Russian shelling of Ukrainians.

The Ukrinform correspondent was told in the Canadian-Ukrainian Foundation(Puzz)which co -finance the medical mission.

“In the city hospital of the Polish city, the mission of Canadian plastic surgeons Cusap began, which operates Ukrainian patients with heavy faces. All patients are victims of war, they have suffered injuries to turmoil weapons and explosions as a result of Russian aggression, ”Ufundia said.

It is noted that within two weeks of surgery will be performed 48 Ukrainian patients who have undergone a preliminary remote examination by Canadian doctors. “Most patients require complex post -traumatic reconstruction of traumatic trauma, soft tissue injuries, upper and lower -end injuries," organization.

Read also: Operations will be expected to take place in three operating rooms, in which surgical crews will work at the same time. “The duration of operations from 5 to 15 hours depending on the severity of the injury. Some Patients Canadian Operate for the second time or third. Postoperation, when the condition of patients stabilizes, will be transported to Ukraine by specialists - also at the expense of the Foundation, ”the Canadian -Ukrainian Foundation was informed.

Surgical teams consist of volunteer health workers from different Canada provinces: nine surgeons, five anesthesiologists, four therapists and 23 nurses. "Each surgical team includes mumultydisciplinary staff, surgical equipment and all the necessary surgical material," Kuf says.

The educational component is also important in the mission of Canadian doctors. “Ukrainian surgeons who are trained in Ukanadian colleagues are invited. Educational seminar of the stretch-line surgery was developed for them. 15 Ukrainian doctors will also take part in this year's mission, ”the foundation assured. Read also: surgeon From 2014 to 2020, the Canadian Mission of Plastic Surgeons was based on the UKIiv Military Hospital, and Canadian doctors also had traffic operations of Ulvo and Odessa. During the work of the mission in Ukraine, the Canadian-Ukrainian Foundation has been able to equip the Kiev military hospital for almost $ 2 million.

This year's mission - the tenth since 2014 and the third, which will take place in Poland, the beginning of a full -scale Russian invasion. Two preliminary missions were in September and November 2022.

All three of the last missions are funded by the donor support collected by the Uramita "Humanitarian Call of Ukraine", which jointly implement the Kanad-Ukrainian Foundation and the Congress of Ukrainians in Canada.

Type: Article

Measures that will help reduce tax revenues or destroy the existing tax base will limit Ukraine to the ability of Ukraine to achieve development goals, which has a mastered impact on long -term economic growth.

According to Ukrinform, a permanent representative of the International Drawing Fund stated it(IMF)In Ukraine, Vagram Stepanian in an interview .

"International community is ready to divide part of the burden, but Ukraine is continuing to fulfill its part and strengthen the mobilization of internal incomes to finance the growing social and infrastructure. The existing tax base, the restriction of Ukraine's ability to achieve the goals of reconstruction and development, which is negative for long -term economic growth, "he said.

Read also: IMF Stepanian stressed that the restoration and reconstruction of Ukraine needed financial resources, as evidenced by a recent assessment of the loss of the tap.

The IMF representative explained that the advanced funding of Ukraine is directed to promoting sustainable and reliable economic growth, which depends on many policy tools.

According to Stepanian, one of these tools is tax policy, since effective and fair tax policy allows to redistribute state resources to meet social and infrastructure needs by the country's simultaneous increase in competitiveness by ensuring equal terms for business. These important functions of tax policy contribute to economic growth, both in general and in the case of Ukraine.

He also noted that the national income strategy, which will be implemented on the program, will help to reconcile the mobilization of revenues with government -proof development and medium -term expenses, including reconstruction and social needs.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-01T15:40:45+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T15:40:45+03:00

Description: The government intends to increase the amount of compensation for employers for employment of persons with disabilities and to make compensation for their workplace. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16829..."]

Tags: ['Інвалідність', 'Компенсація', 'Уряд', 'Робота']

Type: Article

Governments intend to increase the amount of compensation for employers for employment for persons with disabilities and to make compensation for their workplace.

This was announced during the roundtable "Employment of People with Disabilities: European Perspectives in Ukraine" at the Media Center "Ukraine - Ukrinform" by Deputy Minister of Economy of Ukraine Tatiana Berezhna.

“The existing employers' promotion program that involves compensation for a person with a disability of 50% of labor costs, but not more than UAH 6,700, is hardly used by employers. Because it is consumed for persons who are officially registered with employment centers. And there are very few such people among all the unemployed: in that year, their share was only 5.7%. Therefore, the Ministry of Economy has prepared a project that proposes to disseminate a range of programs for employers for integration into the labor market not just officials from among persons with ”, - said the Deputy Minister.

In particular, the procedure for compensation for the arrangement of a workplace for persons with the first and second group of disability is developed.

“These will be rather high in size. Thus, for the arranged working place of people with disabilities of the first group it is proposed to return up to 15 size mining wages, which is just over 100 thousand UAH. As for the second group, it is about the amount of compensation in 10 minimum wages, ”Berezhna stressed.

Read also: with disabilities It is also planned to launch a program similar to the existing, from compensation for the factic costs of wages, taxes and ESAs, but already in the amount of 15 thousand UAH. This program will spread to employers who will employ all persons with disabilities, not just those who have the status of unemployed.

“It is about compensation for up to 15 thousand UAH for six months, which includes the cost of wages, taxes and ESAs. The new programmable to relate to all persons with disabilities, not just those registered with employment, ”the Deputy Minister emphasized.

Type: Article

The prosecutor's office through the court contributed to the introduction of a unified in Ukraine, the current forge in Ukraine in the State Register of Real Estate.

About it reports in The Transcarpathian Regional Prosecutor's Office, Ukrinform reports. h

"The Khust District Prosecutor's Office ensured the execution of all -Khumov for the introduction of a unique gamora water forge to the State Registur Accurable Monuments of Ukraine. For this purpose she filed a lawsuit with the Administrative Administrative Court, which was satisfied there.

It is the only existing water forge in Ukraine, located in the village. Lisichov Nahustshchyna. The fate of the object is under the care of tenants who support the tasks of the work cycle.

It is noted that the registration of the forge in the mentioned register will give it an official statusatus of the monument, which will be protected by the state.

The prosecutor found that the executive committee of the local self -government body did not comply with the requirements of the legislation on the preparation of accounting documentation on the emphasis on local cultural heritage. In addition, he did not submit the proposals to the Higher Level cultural heritage protection - the Department of Culture, Nationalities and Religions of the Transcarpathian Ova - on the introduction of the monument of the State Register of Real Estate Monuments of Ukraine.

Read also: Even after the intervention of the prosecutor's office and the court decision, the executive committee prepared the documentation and appealed to the regional military administration. We consider that all these steps create a legal basis for the protection of the target of the cultural heritage object.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T16:59:38+03:00

Description: The State Border Service refutes information about the murder of a bear in Transcarpathia: it is said that the photo on social networks - found by a border outfit of the corpse of the male bear on the area of the border unit "Kamiannytsky" of the Chop detachment. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16755..."]

Tags: ['Прикордонники', 'Ведмідь', 'Закарпаття']

Type: Article

The Dozhnaya Border Service refutes information about the murder of the Transcarpathian bear: in the photo on social networks - found by the border corpse of the male bear on the area of the border unit "Kamyanitsa" of the Chop detachment.

This was reported in Western Regional Directorate of the State Tax Service of Ukraine, Ukrinform reports.

"This morning on social networks there was information about illegalization in the border in the territory of Uzhany National Park, which seemed to have led to the death of a wild animal( )and possible involvement in this employees of the State Border Guard Service of Ukraine. Given the wide -voice, which this publication has acquired, the leadership of the Chop Border Guard took immediate measures to check the information set out on social networks, its accuracy, as well as all the circumstances of the event. It should be noted that the information is not true, " - the message reads.

As it is currently established, in the beginning of April this year, a border guard found a corpse of a maleweddy on the area of the border unit "Kamianitsa" of the Chop detachment, not a bear, which is confirmed by the relevant act.

According to the SSSU, the head of the border unit informed about the detection of the beast body of the border unit. The last arrival of the place of detection of a dead animal and in the presence of border guards convinced the natural death of the bear. After that, the foresters buried the corpse of the animal, which is confirmed by the relevant act, which also specifies the transmission of signs of gunshot wounds.

Separately, the DPSU noted that the distance from the place where the bear's body was found is about 60 kilometers from the area where the servicemen of the Stuzhitsa department were previously found a bear, which was discussed in a post of representative of the Uzhuzhan National Park.

For full objectivity and establishment of all circumstances, the management of the Chop Border Detachment conducts an official investigation. The National Police and Kamyanitsky Forestry, and Border Guards, were also at the scene.

In view of the situation, the SPSU is not asked to rush with the conclusions and unburdened unverified information before the completion of the audience.

The results of the investigation at the SSSU are promised to report additionally.As it was reported, earlier the head of the State Protection Department of the Uzhansky Park Vladislav Kamenz published a post on Facebook and photos of men of border guards near the Dead Bear.

According to the Uzhan National Park, according to their information, they should believe that the bear was destroyed as a result of illegally designed and carried out and carried out by officials of the State Tax Administration of Ukraine.

On April 16, a bear was found in the territory of the former Veliko Berezny district, which was assaled to Domashin village. It was handed over to the employees of the Uzhansky National Park, and those, in turn, transferred it for rehabilitation to the center of rehabilitation of the bear "Synevyr". After rehabilitation, the bear is promised to be reinforced into the wild.

According to Ukrinform, the press service reports .

  • consequences of a full -scale war, strengthening the role of energy security and strengthening the stability of the power system; * results(Enzo-e)and deepening the integration of Ukraine's energy system into pan -European; * availability of the latest technologies(production and use of hydrogen, small modular nuclear reactors, energy storage facilities), technical changes in the energy sector, world trends and innovative decisions, environmental safety requirements in accordance with EU norms and Ukraine's obligations; * Ukraine's international obligations on energy efficiency and use of RES, reduction of greenhouse gas emissions, etc.; * Decentralization of electricity generation throughout the country.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-01T19:00:27+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T19:00:27+03:00

Description: Bill No. 9165 will allow the State Fund of Regional Development to the projects of the regions that have been most affected by hostilities, and also enables Ukrainians to choose them with the help of "Action" application. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16701..."]

Tags: ['Тергромада', 'Додаток “ДІЯ”']

Type: Article

Bill No. 9165 will allow the State Fund of the Regional Development to the projects of the regions that were most affected by hostilities, and also enables Ukrainians to choose them with the help of "Action" application.

This was reported by the Deputy Minister of Community Development, Territories of Tainfrastructure Alexander Azarchin, Ukrinform reports with a reference to the Ministry's Postering Service .

«У 2022 році ДФРР був призупинений, у цьому році ми маємо адаптувати цейважливий інструмент до реалій воєнного часу та потреб найбільш постраждалихвід російської агресії громад. Законопроєкт зберігає логіку ДФРР, яка буланапрацьована у попередні роки, однак на фініші ми пропонуємо застосуватиінструмент прямої демократії – голосування за проєкти безпосередньогромадянами у Дії», - зазначила вона.

Читайте також: Azarchin said that the previous standards for the distribution of funds of the DFRR took into account the population in the region and the gross regional product indicator, now these indicators are not relevant in wartime. Therefore, the draft law proposals from UAH 2 billion of the DFRD in 2023 to distribute 50% to equal parts between all regions, and the remaining 50% - additionally equal parts of the interior of the111 regions that were most affected by hostilities.

It is envisaged that central and local executive authorities and bodies of self -government will be able to submit projects at the expense of the DFRR through a specialized platform, after which the regional commissions will carry out a premium. It will take place with a point system; Small cities projects will get an additional score with up to 50,000 people.

Projects, which have scored at least 25 points, transfer the Ministry of Investigation Commission, which checks them for compliance with the law and submits for an open survey in action. According to the results of the survey, the lists of wins, which will be submitted by the Cabinet of Ministers for the distribution of DFRR funds will be formed.

As it was reported, on April 11, the Verkhovna Rada approved in the first reading of the law No. 9165 on amendments to the Law of Ukraine "On the State Budget of Ukraine for 2023" on the use of funds of the State Fund of Regional Development.

The International Monetary Fund has planned frequent views of the Extended Financing Program of Ukraine(EFF): one summer and one autumn.

According to Ukrinform, a permanent representative of the International Drawing Fund stated it(IMF)In Ukraine, Vagram Stepanyan in "The Fund's programs are evaluated by regular views involving the IMF experts that are updating their macroeconomic forecasts and bases on the basis of recent data and events, as well as discussing politics with the authorities. We have planned frequent views: one summer and one in the fall," He told.

Stepanian noted that the EFF program was designed to solve the problem of payment balance of Ukraine and the restoration of medium -term foreign life capacity both in the base and pessimistic scenario. That is why financial guarantees for maintaining debt sustainability are also provided for basic tapsimistic scenarios. These requirements meet the Fund's policy of the Foundation in conditions of extremely high uncertainty.

Read also: IMF The IMF representative added that the Foundation prescribed two scenarios of economic development: optimistic and pessimistic. At the same time, a detailed discussion of the mysterious scenario of development of the situation is a necessary feature of the mechanism of mechanism.

"As for the optimistic scenario, we recognize in our assessment of the situation that Ukraine's economic prospects may be more favorable, with a faster termination . And, of course, we all look forward to making economic prospects, "Stepanian explained.

He noted that under the EFF program, the Ukrainian authorities have undertaken to protect and continue reforms to strengthen the government and strengthen the anti -corruption program, including by implementing legislative changes. This sphere is an important part of the program.

Type: Article

Measures that will help reduce tax revenues or destroy the existing tax base will limit Ukraine to the ability of Ukraine to achieve development goals, which has a mastered impact on long -term economic growth.

According to Ukrinform, a permanent representative of the International Drawing Fund stated it(IMF)In Ukraine, Vagram Stepanian in an interview .

"International community is ready to divide part of the burden, but Ukraine is continuing to fulfill its part and strengthen the mobilization of internal incomes to finance the growing social and infrastructure. The existing tax base, the restriction of Ukraine's ability to achieve the goals of reconstruction and development, which is negative for long -term economic growth, "he said.

Read also: IMF Stepanian stressed that the restoration and reconstruction of Ukraine needed financial resources, as evidenced by a recent assessment of the loss of the tap.

The IMF representative explained that the advanced funding of Ukraine is directed to promoting sustainable and reliable economic growth, which depends on many policy tools.

According to Stepanian, one of these tools is tax policy, since effective and fair tax policy allows to redistribute state resources to meet social and infrastructure needs by the country's simultaneous increase in competitiveness by ensuring equal terms for business. These important functions of tax policy contribute to economic growth, both in general and in the case of Ukraine.

He also noted that the national income strategy, which will be implemented on the program, will help to reconcile the mobilization of revenues with government -proof development and medium -term expenses, including reconstruction and social needs.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-05-01T20:49:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-05-01T20:49:00+03:00

Images: ["630_360_16829...", "1682969799-31...", "1682969799-56...", "1682969798-21..."]

Tags: ['Канада', 'Операція', 'Польща', 'Україна', 'Травма']

Type: Article

Leading plastic surgeons will operate in a hospital in southern Poland wounded by Russian shelling of Ukrainians.

The Ukrinform correspondent was told in the Canadian-Ukrainian Foundation(Puzz)which co -finance the medical mission.

“In the city hospital of the Polish city, the mission of Canadian plastic surgeons Cusap began, which operates Ukrainian patients with heavy faces. All patients are victims of war, they have suffered injuries to turmoil weapons and explosions as a result of Russian aggression, ”Ufundia said.

It is noted that within two weeks of surgery will be performed 48 Ukrainian patients who have undergone a preliminary remote examination by Canadian doctors. “Most patients require complex post -traumatic reconstruction of traumatic trauma, soft tissue injuries, upper and lower -end injuries," organization.

Read also: Operations will be expected to take place in three operating rooms, in which surgical crews will work at the same time. “The duration of operations from 5 to 15 hours depending on the severity of the injury. Some Patients Canadian Operate for the second time or third. Postoperation, when the condition of patients stabilizes, will be transported to Ukraine by specialists - also at the expense of the Foundation, ”the Canadian -Ukrainian Foundation was informed.

Surgical teams consist of volunteer health workers from different Canada provinces: nine surgeons, five anesthesiologists, four therapists and 23 nurses. "Each surgical team includes mumultydisciplinary staff, surgical equipment and all the necessary surgical material," Kuf says.

The educational component is also important in the mission of Canadian doctors. “Ukrainian surgeons who are trained in Ukanadian colleagues are invited. Educational seminar of the stretch-line surgery was developed for them. 15 Ukrainian doctors will also take part in this year's mission, ”the foundation assured. Read also: surgeon From 2014 to 2020, the Canadian Mission of Plastic Surgeons was based on the UKIiv Military Hospital, and Canadian doctors also had traffic operations of Ulvo and Odessa. During the work of the mission in Ukraine, the Canadian-Ukrainian Foundation has been able to equip the Kiev military hospital for almost $ 2 million.

This year's mission - the tenth since 2014 and the third, which will take place in Poland, the beginning of a full -scale Russian invasion. Two preliminary missions were in September and November 2022.

All three of the last missions are funded by the donor support collected by the Uramita "Humanitarian Call of Ukraine", which jointly implement the Kanad-Ukrainian Foundation and the Congress of Ukrainians in Canada.

Illustrative photo

The Minister of Defense of Ukraine Alexei Reznikov told about it in an interview with Tandriy Tsaplienko on the air of the Teleterna "Unified News".

He noted that there are three lines of service and repair. First of all, it is a minor repair.

  • Crews and techniques of Ukrainian units are trained and know how to do it. The task is to provide them with spare parts. We are already producing some spare parts for Western equipment in the Ukrainian market - both in state and most enterprises.

The second repair line is a more complex, medium level of complexity, which can be fulfilled at Ukrainian enterprises located at a certain distance of the front of the front, in those cities where there are industrial capabilities.

  • Our engineers and techniques have learned to make such repairs. But here also requires copies, drawings, engineering documents, so we constantly conduct negotiations about permits, licenses and more.

If necessary, in a difficult repair that concerns electronics or something, the equipment is forced to send abroad. To carry out it built a hub in partner countries.

-For example, about Leopard 2 tanks, we have signed a memorandum on the previous Ramstinna together with Germany's Defense Minister and Viceremier-Minister of the Polish National Defense Minister of Poland on the creation of a hab of repair in Poland. VPK will set up to deploy its production capacity there. Every day we work over the main task - a constant, unobstructed, uninterrupted restoration of technology, - said Alexei Reznikov.

About it reportsThe press service of the National Police of Ukraine.

On March 5, the Russian soldiers established fire control over Olegakoshov Street on departure from Irpin. This is the only road that could be used to transport from the city.

The next day, at 7:30, the locals began to leave the city on cars, on which the postcards with the inscriptions "Children" and "Evacuation" were glued. The column was moving the Unapryamka of the Zhytomyr highway.

The occupier shot the first car - Jeep Patriot, in which the couple was traveling. The water was injured. The serviceman under the sight of the automatic assaulting them to the captured premises for questioning. Meanwhile, the Evacuation Column of cars moved down the street, on which the sergeant, along with other collectors, opened fire from grenade launchers and small arms.

The Russians shot 6 cars: five peaceful people were killed, seven more wounded, including a child.

Military criminals were very cruel to seriously wounded, and they had the opportunity to assist them. People were lying on the ground and dying. Those who could go on their own - were driven to the enthusiastic house for about two hours under the muzzle.

The guilt of the paratrooper of the Russian army is confirmed by the testimony of the victims of the trusted atrocities over the inhabitants of Irpen.

In an exclusive comment on the correspondent Armyinform, the official said that communication remains one of our main problems:

  • Ukrainians who have unique ideas that could significantly strengthen the domestic defense sector are not always well informed. Read also:

In Ukraine launched a defense technology development cluster Brave 1 The Ministry of Defense of Ukraine, as a component of this ecosystem, has worked and will work to accelerate this process, starting from the moment of seizure of pilot projects to the department to codification, ending with the issuance of the order of operation.To contribute, that to evaluate the importance of the latest proposals from Ukrainian inventors and developers will be specialists from a specially formed group of experts under the Brave1 platform. ** It has already included 556 specialists not only . Tsedulying institutes, we also have a section of the National Academy of Sciences. We are working with universities on military topics. We have a large representation in this expert group, - says Vladimir Gavrilov.

According to him, the leading task at the previous stage of formation of such a group of defense technologies is to find qualified experts who have quickly evaluated, to what category to attribute the idea that comes. For example, if there is a high appraisal category, if there is already a prototype of the product, then it is possible to run into a short category of admission to operation. Or, on the contrary, low, where, in addition to the idea, there is nothing more, and you need to help personally through grants to bring the project to the prototype. And there is already a whole mechanism Brave1 - with their grants, additional examinations and the industrial sites of the Ministry of Social Policy and the Ministry of Economy. And when the prototypes for the Ministry of Defense will be answered, these projects will be all -folding the examination. And then there will be only an accelerator of the Ministry of Defense, which will quickly be armed. This accelerator will be planned to be introduced this week. And it is part of this ecosystem.

According to Deputy Minister of Defense Volodymyr Gavrilov, one of the main calls and tasks of the Brave1 platform is the protection of copyright inventors.

In Ukraine, the industry of prostheses needs serious reform - Mikhail Tsymbalyuk

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-05-01T81:00:00-04:00

Description: Opzy delka Tyesyach Gromyan Ukrainian to prove for prosthetics, Yaki is simpler Varo -preparation ... Images: ['photo_5368576251347978249_y.jpg']

Tags: ['ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ПРОТЕЗУВАННЯ', 'СОЦЗАХИСТ ПІД ЧАС ВІЙНИ']

Category: News

Currently, several thousand citizens of Ukraine are expecting prostheses that are easy to prepare and serve domestic specialists. According to current law, all prosthetics in Ukraine are free of charge. And this is very important to those citizens who doubt today whether a prosthesis is worth establishing. Here the answer should be unambiguous - worth it.

—The ballow of prostheses requires serious reform, because it has been released to the background, several important conditions of Ukraine were closed: Kyiv, Lviv, Ternopil, Cherkasy. The current state has planned more budgetary funds for 2023, because several citizens of Ukraine, especially servicemen, are expected to be prosthetized - notedThe first deputy chairman of the Verkhovna Rada of Ukraine Committee on Social Policy and the Protection of Veterans Rights Mykhailo Tsymbalyuk.

This year in the state budget for prosthetics there are more than UAH 356 million(Last year - less than UAH 24 million). Загалом у 2023 на реабілітаціювійськових заплановано понад 2,5 млрд грн. Окрім протезів, кошти підуть напротезно-ортопедичні вироби, спеціальні засоби для самообслуговування тазасоби для пересування.

Михайло Цимбалюк наголосив на необхідності розвитку саме вітчизняної галузіпротезування, зокрема, що нам потрібні добре підготовлені лікарі та бригадиреабілітологів, здатні місяцями працювати над відновленням людини післявстановлення протеза.

— Коли ми звертаємося по допомогу до міжнародних партнерів, громадяни Українимають кілька місяців перебувати за кордоном з метою протезування. Ба більше, умайбутньому протези потребують обслуговування, а якщо протез встановлений закордоном, то громадянину доведеться виїжджати туди, витрачати кошти і час, —пояснив він.

Однозначно більш доцільно встановлювати протез, освоювати його та проходитиреабілітаційний курс у вітчизняних центрах протезування, вважає МихайлоЦимбалюк. В Україні працюють як державні, так і приватні реабілітаційніцентри, тож можна проаналізувати пропозиції і обрати — послуги з протезуваннябезкоштовні.

One of the problems of prosthetics is bureaucratized in communication between those who need prosthetics and government agencies.

  • In fact, there is a problem, because when a person loses his limb, it is antening psychologically, so it is important that the local governments, the regulatory structures of the Ministry of Social Policy are not waiting for the citizen or citizen to talk to them, and they did the corresponding work themselves, - said Mykolacibalyuk. - It is important that people know where to go and not waste time, because the recovery period, from the beginning of the prosthesis and dosing, lasts from three to six months. It is a difficult process, and the more it begins, the more complex the future rehabilitation.

We will remind, a serviceman who has a certificate of injury(Even if it is not yet issued a disability), is entitled to free receipt of the prosthesis regardless of the number of amputations.

The state prosthetics procedure is currently quite complicated, it provides for series. According to her now, the action algorithm is as follows:

First, the injured person must choose a prosthetic enterprise on his own, and it is difficult to use if you have never encountered it: not just evaluate the technical possible, providing appropriate personnel and honesty of the enterprise, giving prosthetics services.

Secondly, after the choice of the contractor, a contract with a prosthetic enterprise is signed, and it, for its part, concludes an agreement on the Ministry of Social Policy.

Among the existing problems, the most common is prosthetics delay. Usually, it may be due to the fact that businesses do not start work until the budget is received. On the other hand, if the enterprise does not have sufficient production capabilities, then the term of production of the prosthesis can also be delayed. Therefore, you should not delay and seek the prosthetics as soon as possible.

_ Prepared Lesia Medvedenko_

Images: ['ecd26821cc87b12d6493e5de862ed896.jpeg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ІПСО РФ', 'СБУ']

Category: News

Cyberfachivtsi of the Security Service together with Babs blocked in Poltava a powerful proxide-center, which the aggressor used for the subversive activity of anti-Ukraine.

About it reportsSBU.

As a result of complex measures, the organizers of illegality were detained. They were two residents of Poltava and Kharkiv regions.

Dilles set up an underground proxy center that worked as a VPN service. Windows to make subscribers from any country to produce themselves for users of Ukrainian mobile Internet.

The cost of such "subscription" was almost UAH 2.5 thousand per month.

According to operational information, the persons who received hundreds of "orders" daily, Agroshi received through prohibited payment systems.

Among the "regular" clients were citizens of the Russian Federation who, through proxy services, hid their own IP addresses for access to popular social networks.

At the same time, the servers of the enemy "cell" were in the territory of the aggressor country.

This allowed the Russian special services to receive remote access of the D-Ukrainian Internet Space, as well as to distribute the Kremlin narratives of Taufaya information about the situation on the front allegedly on behalf of Ukrainian citizens.

During the searches at the places of stay of the attackers found:

  • special hardware complex; * $ 120 thousand and half a kilogram of gold; * mobile phones and draft records with evidence of illegal activity.

The United States has been organizing three successful evacuation convoy days, so that exported persons, including citizens of other countries, covered with Hartum's armed conflict to Port-Sudan.

Images: ["630_360_16829..."]

Tags: None

Type: Article

Last week, two Canadian volunteers were killed in Bakhmut's battles, who served as a vintational legion.

About it reports Canadian public broadcaster , reports Ukrinform.

"The 27-year-old Kayle Porter resident and 21-year-old Zelenko from Misaasent-Ketrins served in the Ukrainian International Legion,"-said.

It is noted that on the evening of April 26, when Canadian volunteers together with the Ukrainian military were involved in a combat operation on the maintenance of the clad route of supply to Bakhmut, they were covered by the Artillery Fire of the Russian Federation.

“Porter, Zelenko and at least three Ukrainian military found shelters in a fortified bunker, but he has suffered a direct hit. Everyone was killed, ”CBC News rejoices with reference to the commander of servicemen.

According to the newspaper, Porter and Zelenko used to served in the Armed Forces, but resigned before joining the Ukrainian boarding legion. "According to their commander, two were marsed by close friends," the publication indicates.

As it is specified, the body of Zelenko has already been found and delivered to Kharkiv, and the body was still looking for.

The Coordination Headquarters met with the families of prisoners of orchestrants of the36th Separate Marine Infantry Brigade named after Mikhail Bilynsky.

Representatives of the coordination headquarters, the National Police, the Security Service of Ukraine and the Office of the Commissioner of the Verkhovna Rights Council answered the questions.

About it reportsCoordinating headquarters for the issue of prisoners of war.

“They discussed the health of our defenders and defenders in captivity. Many people have been in captivity for more than a year without proper medical care. Ukraine is doing everything to return them home and make the aggressor country guarantee the necessary condition. But this, unfortunately, depends not only on Ukraine, ”the presentation says.

However, for the ICRC International Community, it is evidence of our people's enslavement and violation of the agreements on their release.

The relatives were also interested in whether it was possible to re-select DNA.

  • Sometimes there is poor first selection of DNA. But such cases are isolated, ”the police representative.

Also, with the representative of the Office of the Commissioner of the Verkhovna Rada of Human Rights, they were naming how to raise the problem of torture at the international level and the improper conditions of keeping our prisoners in Russia.
